msg:The location is in the center of the island. It is very convenient to go wherever you go. The hotel environment is very tidy and clean. It looks very high-end. The lady at the front desk is very beautiful and gentle and patient. Any questions will be answered at any time. The most important thing is the large lake in the room. The scenery is also very beautiful. I was exhausted after a day of playing. I came back to take a shower and I was very satisfied with the water flow. I will definitely come here next time! !

msg:Personally feel that it is not worth the price. After all, it is a Lakeview Ctrip 5-diamond hotel:
1. The rooms are very empty on the day of check-in, but the waiter is still arranged on the 4th floor. You need to walk to the public balcony to see the lake. The room is still directly opposite the elevator (but the public balcony has a lot of tables and chairs, which is good)
2. After all, the old Bailuzhou Hotel was renovated and the room size is very small
3. The material of the shower room in the bathroom is very cheap, the water will still seep out when the glass door is closed, making the whole bathroom very wet
4. The air-conditioning and refrigeration are very general. It is suspected that the central air-conditioning in the hotel has controlled the cooling temperature. It was turned on strongly at 17 degrees and it was turned on for an afternoon. The temperature in the room still showed 24 degrees.
5. It's the air conditioning problem. No matter how low the wind is, the sound of the air conditioning exhaust fan is very loud (but the air output is small), which greatly affects the experience of staying (especially when I am mentally weak and difficult to fall asleep)
6. The hotelâ€™s front desk security/service is lacking. The lobby is empty around 12 AM. I canâ€™t find anyone when I want to find someone in the lobby. The door of the security room inside is open. The front desk clerk is looking for a long time to come
Can only say that the same price is not recommended
